# Trusted Bums Codex Edit Log

_Last updated: 2026-06-19 by Codex._

This file is the running handoff log for implementation work Codex has made in this repo. Specialist agents should read it before preserving backlog items so they can recheck shipped changes, downgrade stale recommendations, and add only the remaining gaps.

## Log Protocol

- Append a new dated entry after every Codex implementation or pushed handoff.
- Include the commit or branch when available, the user request, the files or surfaces changed, checks run, and specialist agents that should recheck the work.
- Do not paste secrets, raw private data, credential values, or mailbox contents.
- If a pushed commit included pre-existing dirty files outside the current implementation scope, call that out instead of implying Codex authored every line.

### 2026-06-15 - Fix Bing canonical URL mismatch

- Trigger: Ryan challenged the zero Bing traffic result because direct visits and daily QA should show up somewhere.
- Diagnosis: Bing Webmaster traffic is search-result traffic, so direct visits and QA runs do not count. However, the deeper Bing API review found a real crawl/indexing issue: `GetUserSites` verified only `https://trustedbums.com/`, `GetCrawlStats` showed only `1` URL in index, `GetUrlInfo` showed the homepage crawled but `/bums`, legal, and privacy URLs with default/empty crawl dates, and production served sitemap URLs such as `/bums` through a `301` to `/bums/` while the final page declared canonical `/bums`. That sitemap/redirect/canonical mismatch was likely weakening Bing’s ability to consolidate and index the non-home public pages.
- What changed: Updated public route canonical generation so generated route snapshots and runtime metadata use the trailing-slash URL that production actually serves. Updated `public/sitemap.xml` to list trailing-slash public URLs and refreshed `lastmod` to `2026-06-16`. Updated IndexNow and Bing Webmaster URL submission helpers to submit the 13 search-indexable public URLs with trailing slashes and to stop submitting `/login`.
- Main surfaces changed: `src/data/publicRouteMetadata.ts`, `src/components/RouteMetadata.tsx`, `scripts/render-route-metadata.mjs`, `scripts/bing-webmaster-api.mjs`, `scripts/submit-indexnow.mjs`, `public/sitemap.xml`, and this edit log.
- Checks run: Bing API diagnostic calls for `GetUserSites`, `GetRankAndTrafficStats`, `GetFeeds`, `GetQueryStats`, `GetPageStats`, `GetCrawlStats`, `GetCrawlIssues`, `GetUrlSubmissionQuota`, `GetUrlInfo`, and `GetUrlTrafficInfo`; Bingbot `curl` checks for the homepage, `/bums`, legal, and privacy routes; `VITE_CLERK_PUBLISHABLE_KEY=pk_test_dummy VITE_SUPABASE_URL=https://vaoqvtxqvbptyxddpoju.supabase.co VITE_SUPABASE_ANON_KEY=dummy VITE_GOOGLE_ANALYTICS_MEASUREMENT_ID=G-P6B5EYQMVN VITE_MICROSOFT_CLARITY_PROJECT_ID=x7nevilplm corepack pnpm run build`; `corepack pnpm exec vitest run src/test/scrumQueueRegression.test.ts src/test/microsoftClarityConsent.test.tsx src/test/googleAnalyticsConsent.test.tsx src/test/analyticsEvents.test.ts`; `corepack pnpm exec tsc --noEmit --pretty false`; `node scripts/submit-indexnow.mjs --dry-run`; and `node scripts/bing-webmaster-api.mjs health`.
- Results: Local build now renders `https://trustedbums.com/bums/` and `https://trustedbums.com/legal/terms-of-service/` as matching canonical and `og:url` values. The sitemap now lists 13 trailing-slash search URLs. The dry-run IndexNow payload also lists those 13 trailing-slash URLs. Production still needs this change deployed before resubmitting sitemap/URLs to Bing.

- Results: CEO risk-taking is now intentional rather than accidental.
